## Diagram 2

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Created
    Created --> InTransit: origin_departed
    InTransit --> AtDestination: destination_arrived
    AtDestination --> Delivered: delivery_confirmed
    InTransit --> Delayed: delay_detected
    Delayed --> InTransit: delay_resolved
    Delivered --> [*]
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Initialize PackageContainer] --> B{Set Attributes}
    B --> C[solution_id]
    B --> D[tracking_number]
    B --> E[description]
    B --> F[lifecycle_state]
    B --> G[status]
    B --> H[timestamps]
    B --> I[location_codes]
    B --> J[trip_leg_ids]
    C --> K[add_dirty_field]
    D --> K
    E --> K
    F --> K
    G --> K
    H --> K
    I --> K
    J --> K
    K --> L{is_valid?}
    L -->|Yes| M[to_dict]
    L -->|No| N[Return False]
    M --> O[Persist to Database]
```
